Rebuild store-day exog residual\nsales=[]\nfor f in sorted(glob.glob('sales_transaction_*.csv')):\n    df=pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['store_id','product_id','sales_date','units_sold','revenue','promo_price'],parse_dates=['sales_date'])\n    sales.append(df.groupby(['store_id','sales_date']).agg(revenue=('revenue','sum'),units=('units_sold','sum'),promo_lines=('promo_price',lambda s:(s>0).sum()),lines=('product_id','count')).reset_index().rename(columns={'sales_date':'date'}))\nX=pd.concat(sales,ignore_index=True); X['promo_line_share']=X.promo_lines/X.lines\ntraffic=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f,parse_dates=['traffic_date']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('store_traffic_*.csv'))],ignore_index=True).rename(columns={'traffic_date':'date'})\nX=X.merge(traffic[['store_id','date','customer_count']],on=['store_id','date'],how='left')\n# store promos\npromos=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('store_promotion_*.csv'))],ignore_index=True); X['log_traffic']=np.log1p(X.customer_count); X['log_size']=np.log1p(X.store_size_sqm); X['traffic_per_sqm']=X.customer_count/X.store_size_sqm; X['month']=X.date.dt.month.astype(str); X['dow']=X.date.dt.dayofweek.astype(str)\nfeatures_num=['log_traffic','log_size','traffic_per_sqm','promo_line_share','store_promo_lines','display_active_lines','avg_discounted_price']\nfeatures_cat=['store_type','location','region','month','dow']\npipe=make_pipeline(ColumnTransformer([('num',StandardScaler(),features_num),('cat',OneHotEncoder(handle_unknown='ignore'),features_cat)]),Ridge(alpha=1.0))\npipe.fit(X[features_num+features_cat],X.log_revenue); X['resid']=X.log_revenue-pipe.predict(X[features_num+features_cat])\nstore_res=X.groupby(['rep_id','store_id']).resid.mean().reset_index()\nglobal_sd=store_res.resid.std(ddof=1)\nrep=store_res.groupby('rep_id').agg(mean=('resid','mean'), sd=('resid','std'), count=('resid','size')).reset_index()\nrep['se_global']=global_sd/np.sqrt(5); rep['z_global']=rep['mean']/rep['se_global']; rep['p_one']=norm.cdf(rep.z_global)\n# Benjamini Hochberg one-sided\nrep=rep.sort_values('p_one').reset_index(drop=True); rep['rank']=np.arange(1,len(rep)+1); rep['bh_thresh']=rep['rank']/len(rep)*0.05; rep['bh_sig']=rep.p_one<=rep.bh_thresh\nprint('global store residual sd',global_sd,'se',global_sd/np.sqrt(5))\nprint(rep.head(25).to_string(index=False,float_format=lambda v:f'{v:.5g}'))\nprint('BH sig', rep[rep.bh_sig].rep_id.tolist())\n# annual store-level model\nann=X.groupby('store_id').agg(revenue=('revenue','sum'),traffic=('customer_count','sum'),promo_line_share=('promo_line_share','mean'),store_promo_lines=('store_promo_lines','sum'),display_active_lines=('display_active_lines','sum'),avg_discounted_price=('avg_discounted_price','mean')).reset_index().merge(stores,on='store_id').merge(primary,on='store_id')\nann['log_revenue']=np.log1p(ann.revenue); ann['log_traffic']=np.log1p(ann.traffic); ann['log_size']=np.log1p(ann.store_size_sqm); ann['traffic_per_sqm']=ann.traffic/ann.store_size_sqm\nnum=['log_traffic','log_size','traffic_per_sqm','promo_line_share','store_promo_lines','display_active_lines','avg_discounted_price']; cat=['store_type','location','region']\npipe2=make_pipeline(ColumnTransformer([('num',StandardScaler(),num),('cat',OneHotEncoder(handle_unknown='ignore'),cat)]),Ridge(alpha=1.0))\npipe2.fit(ann[num+cat],ann.log_revenue); ann['resid_ann']=ann.log_revenue-pipe2.predict(ann[num+cat])\nprint('annual R2',r2_score(ann.log_revenue,pipe2.predict(ann[num+cat])))\ngsd=ann.resid_ann.std(ddof=1); rep2=ann.groupby('rep_id').agg(mean=('resid_ann','mean'),sd=('resid_ann','std'),count=('resid_ann','size')).reset_index(); rep2['z_global']=rep2['mean']/(gsd/np.sqrt(5)); rep2['p_one']=norm.cdf(rep2.z_global); rep2=rep2.sort_values('p_one').reset_index(drop=True); rep2['rank']=np.arange(1,101); rep2['bh_thresh']=rep2['rank']/100*0.05; rep2['bh_sig']=rep2.p_one<=rep2.bh_thresh\nprint('annual store residual sd',gsd,'se',gsd/np.sqrt(5))\nprint(rep2.head(25).to_string(index=False,float_format=lambda v:f'{v:.5g}'))\nprint('annual BH sig', rep2[rep2.bh_sig].rep_id.tolist())\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
